[30;1m187 | [0m[35m-----[0m
[30;1m188 | [0m[35m* Added support for ``checkpw``, a convenience method for verifying a password.[0m
[30;1m189 | [0m[35m* Ensure that you get a ``$2y$`` hash when you input a ``$2y$`` salt.[0m

[30;1m191 | [0m[35m* Fixed compilation under Alpine Linux.[0m
